2025-10-01T23:58:43.6389660Z [36;1m  while [ $attempt -le $max_attempts ]; do[0m

2025-10-01T23:58:43.6390290Z [36;1m      --entitlements src/build/osx/entitlements.plist \[0m

2025-10-01T23:58:43.6391600Z [36;1m[0m
2025-10-01T23:58:43.6391840Z [36;1m    if [ $attempt -lt $max_attempts ]; then[0m

2025-10-01T23:58:43.6393390Z [36;1m    else[0m
2025-10-01T23:58:43.6393680Z [36;1m      echo "Codesign failed after $max_attempts attempts for $target"[0m
2025-10-01T23:58:43.6394000Z [36;1m      return 1[0m
2025-10-01T23:58:43.6394200Z [36;1m    fi[0m
